# Resource Format Implementation Archives

Consolidated archive of GitHub URL references and implementation notes removed from resource format modules under `Libraries/PyKotor/src/pykotor/resource/formats/`.

Each section preserves the verbatim lines from one source module. For the original scrub workflow, see `scripts/archive_github_url_lines.py`.

---

<a id="bwm_data_github_urls_pre_scrub"></a>

## Archived GitHub URL lines — resource/formats/bwm/bwm_data.py

Verbatim lines removed from Libraries/PyKotor/src/pykotor/resource/formats/bwm/bwm_data.py (KotOR.js / kotorblender walkmesh anchors). Normative: wiki/BWM-File-Format.md.



Canonical upstream and **th3w1zard1** mirror/fork permalinks (`blob` / `tree` + commit) follow [Home](Home) cross-references. Resolved via GitHub API (`master` / `main` tip) on 2026-03-25.

When upstream and mirror SHAs differ, line anchors may not match both trees.

- [ndixUR/mdlops](https://github.com/ndixUR/mdlops)

**Commit SHAs (canonical / mirror):**

- **mdlops:** `7e40846d36acb5118e2e9feb2fd53620c29be540` — upstream and mirror share this tip today (ndixUR and th3w1zard1).

- **KotOR.js:** canonical `ea9491d5c783364cf285f178434b84405bee3608` (KobaltBlu); mirror `0067b672a124bbbdaf4006dd0a5d6c2751523195` (th3w1zard1).

## Archived GitHub URL lines — `resource/formats/vis/vis_data.py`

Verbatim lines removed from `Libraries/PyKotor/src/pykotor/resource/formats/vis/vis_data.py`. See `wiki/reverse_engineering_findings.md`.



Canonical upstream and **th3w1zard1** mirror/fork permalinks (`blob` / `tree` + commit) follow [Home](Home) cross-references. Resolved via GitHub API (`master` / `main` tip) on 2026-03-25.

When upstream and mirror SHAs differ, line anchors may not match both trees.

- (reference)
  - Upstream (KobaltBlu/KotOR.js): <https://github.com/KobaltBlu/KotOR.js/blob/ea9491d5c783364cf285f178434b84405bee3608/src/resource/VISObject.ts#L33-L276>
